# V4.1 toxic narratives

> *Raw extractions of cognitive dissonance and market-induced panic.* 

---

### 🤯 Breakdown: 601869.SH on 2024-06-17 (Action: WAIT)

**Brief Rationale (What the bosses see):**
> ADX 19.4 indicates range-bound market, well below the 25 threshold required for trend confirmation. DI Bull is False with DI- (22.4) slightly higher than DI+ (21.8). Despite today's +1.9% gain, there is no structural trend evidence to justify entry. Will wait for ADX > 25 with DI+ > DI- before considering any position.

**Inner Journal (What she is actually screaming inside):**
> Tempting to see +1.9% today and RSI moving from 44.5 to 50.3 and think something is brewing. But ADX at 19.4? That's weak sauce. The system labels trend_mode as 'acceleration' but ADX clearly says 'no trend'. I've been burned before buying into weak ADX 'breakouts' that turned out to be fakeouts in range markets. My entry rule is clear: ADX > 25 with DI Bull confirmation. Neither condition is met. I'll wait. Let them prove the trend first. If this is real, there will be better entries later with ADX confirmation. Cash is a position too. Patience wins in range markets.
